  \usepackage{fontspec}
  %% redefine some chars (either changed by parsing, or not commonly in font)
  \catcode`⃥=\active \def⃥{\textbackslash}
  \catcode`‿=\active \def‿{\textunderscore}
  \catcode`❴=\active \def❴{\{}
  \catcode`❵=\active \def❵{\}}
  \catcode`〔=\active \def〔{{[}}% translate 〔OPENING TORTOISE SHELL BRACKET
  \catcode`〕=\active \def〕{{]}}% translate 〕CLOSING TORTOISE SHELL BRACKET
  \catcode` =\active \def {\,}
  \catcode`·=\active \def·{\textbullet}
  %% BREAK PERMITTED HERE: \discretionary{-}{}{}\nobreak\hspace{0pt}
  \catcode`=\active \def{\-}
  \catcode`ꣵ=\active \defꣵ{%
  म्\textsuperscript{cb}%for candrabindu
  }
  %% show a lot of tolerance
  \tolerance=9000

  \def\textKorean{\fontspec{Baekmuk Gulim} }

  \newcommand\bo\tibetanfont
  
    \defaultfontfeatures{Scale=MatchLowercase,Mapping=tex-text}
	\setmainfont{TeX Gyre Pagella}
    \setsansfont{TeX Gyre Bonum}
  
  \setmonofont{DejaVu Sans Mono}
	  %% page layout start: fit to a4 and US letterpaper (example in memoir.pdf)
	  %% page layout start
	  % stocksize (actual size of paper in the printer) is a4 as per class
	  % options;
	  
	  % trimming, i.e., which part should be cut out of the stock (this also
	  % sets \paperheight and \paperwidth):
	  % \settrimmedsize{0.9\stockheight}{0.9\stockwidth}{*}
	  % \settrimmedsize{225mm}{150mm}{*}
	  % % say where you want to trim
	  \setlength{\trimtop}{\stockheight}    % \trimtop = \stockheight
	  \addtolength{\trimtop}{-\paperheight} %           - \paperheight
	  \setlength{\trimedge}{\stockwidth}    % \trimedge = \stockwidth
	  \addtolength{\trimedge}{-\paperwidth} %           - \paperwidth
	  % % this makes trims equal on top and bottom (which means you must cut
	  % % twice). if in doubt, cut on top, so that dust won't settle when book
	  % % is in shelf
	  \settrims{0.5\trimtop}{0.5\trimedge}

	  % figure out which font you're using
	  \setxlvchars
	  \setlxvchars
	  % \typeout{LENGTH: lxvchars: \the\lxvchars}
	  % \typeout{LENGTH: xlvchars: \the\xlvchars}

	  % set the size of the text block next:
	  % this sets \textheight and \textwidth (not the whole page including
	  % headers and footers)
	  \settypeblocksize{230mm}{130mm}{*}

	  % left and right margins:
	  % this way spine and edge margins are the same
	  % \setlrmargins{*}{*}{*}
	  \setlrmargins{*}{*}{1.5}

	  % upper and lower, same logic as before
	  % \setulmargins{*}{*}{*}% upper = lower margin
	  % \uppermargin = \topmargin + \headheight + \headsep
	  %\setulmargins{*}{*}{1.5}% 1.5*upper = lower margin
	  \setulmargins{*}{*}{1.5}% 

	  % header and footer spacings
	  \setheadfoot{2\baselineskip}{2\baselineskip}

	  % \setheaderspaces{ headdrop }{ headsep }{ ratio }
	  \setheaderspaces{*}{*}{1.5}

	  % see memman p. 51 for this solution to widows/orphans 
	  \setlength{\topskip}{1.6\topskip}
	  % fix up layout
	  \checkandfixthelayout
	  %% page layout end
	
	  \sloppybottom
	
	    % numbering depth

	    % set up layout of toc

	  \vspace*{\baselineskip}
	  
	      % author(s)

	    {\small  — A SARIT edition}\\[\baselineskip]
	    {\Large SARIT}\\\vspace*{\baselineskip}\plogo\par
	  \vspace*{3\baselineskip}
	  \endgroup
	  \end{english}}

       % simplify what ledmac does with fonts, because it breaks. From the documentation of ledmac:
       % The notes are actually given seven parameters: the page, line, and sub-line num-
       % ber for the start of the lemma; the same three numbers for the end of the lemma;
       % and the font specifier for the lemma.

\chapter[{3.2 dravyasamuddeśaḥ}][{3.2 dravyasamuddeśaḥ}]{3.2 dravyasamuddeśaḥ}

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.2.1 ātmā vastu svabhāvaś ca śarīraṃ tattvam ity api 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	dravyam ity asya paryāyās tac ca nityam iti smṛtam 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.2.2 satyaṃ vastu tadākārair asatyair avadhāryate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	asatyopādhibhiḥ śabdaiḥ satyam evābhidhīyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.2.3 adhruveṇa nimittena devadattagṛhaṃ yathā 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	gṛhītaṃ gṛhaśabdena śuddham evābhidhīyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.2.4 suvarṇādi yathā yuktaṃ svair ākārair apāyibhiḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	rucakādyabhidhānānāṃ śuddham evaiti vācyatām 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.2.5 ākāraiś ca vyavacchedāt sārvārthyam avarudhyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	yathaiva cakṣurādīnāṃ sāmarthyaṃ nālikādibhiḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.2.6 teṣv ākāreṣu yaḥ śabdas tathābhūteṣu vartate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	tattvātmakatvāt tenāpi nityam evābhidhīyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.2.7 na tattvātattvayor bheda iti vṛddhebhya āgamaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	atattvam iti manyante tattvam evāvicāritam 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.2.8 vikalparūpaṃ bhajate tattvam evāvikalpitam 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	na cātra kālabhedo+asti kālabhedaś ca gṛhyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.2.9 yathā viṣayadharmāṇāṃ jñāne+atyantam asaṃbhavaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	tadātmeva ca tat siddham atyantam atadātmakam 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.2.10 tathā vikārarūpāṇāṃ tattve+atyantam asaṃbhavaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	tadātmeva ca tat tattvam atyantam atadātmakam 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par

	3.2.11 sat yam ākṛtisaṃhāre yad ante vyavatiṣṭhate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	tan nityaṃ śabdavācyaṃ tac chabdāt tac ca na bhidyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.2.12 na tad asti na tan nāsti na tad ekaṃ na tat pṛthak 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	na saṃsṛṣṭaṃ vibhaktaṃ na vikṛtaṃ na na cānyathā 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.2.13 tan nāsti vidyate tac ca tad ekaṃ tat pṛthak pṛthak 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	saṃsṛṣṭaṃ ca vibhaktaṃ ca vikṛtaṃ tat tad anyathā 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.2.14 tasya śabdārthasaṃbandha- rūpam ekasya dṛśyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	tad dṛśyaṃ darśanaṃ draṣṭā darśane ca prayojanam 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.2.15 vikārāpagame satyaṃ suvarṇaṃ kuṇḍale yathā 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	vikārāpagame satyāṃ tathāhuḥ prakṛtiṃ parām 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.2.16 vācyā sā sarvaśabdānāṃ śabdāś ca na pṛthak tataḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	apṛthaktve ca saṃbandhas tayor nānātmanor iva 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.2.17 ātmā paraḥ priyo dveṣyo vaktā vācyaṃ prayojanam 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	viruddhāni yathaikasya svapne rūpāṇi cetasaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.2.18 ajanmani tathā nitye paurvāparyavivarjite 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	tattve janmādirūpatvaṃ viruddham upalabhyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	iti dravyasamuddeśaḥ
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par

\chapter[{3.3 saṃbandhasamuddeśaḥ}][{3.3 saṃbandhasamuddeśaḥ}]{ 3.3 saṃbandhasamuddeśaḥ}

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.3.1 jñānaṃ prayoktur bāhyo+arthaḥ svarūpaṃ ca pratīyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	śabdair uccaritais teṣāṃ saṃbandhaḥ samavasthitaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.3.2 pratipattur bhavaty arthe jñāne vā saṃśayaḥ kva cit 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	svarūpeṣūpalabhyeṣu vyabhicāro na vidyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.3.3 asyāyaṃ vācako vācya iti ṣaṣṭhyā pratīyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	yogaḥ śabdārthayos tattvam apy ato vyapadiśyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.3.4 nābhidhānaṃ svadharmeṇa saṃbandhasyāsti vācakam 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	atyantaparatantratvād rūpaṃ nāsyāpadiśyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.3.5 upakārāt sa yatrāsti dharmas tatrānugamyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	śaktīnām api sā śaktir guṇānām apy asau guṇaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.3.6 taddharmaṇos tu tācchabdyaṃ   saṃyogasamavāyayoḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	tayor apy upakārārthā niyatās tadupādhayaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.3.7 kā cid eva hi sāvasthā kāryaprasavasūcitā 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	kasya cit kena cid yasyāṃ saṃyoga upajāyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.3.8 nirātmakānām utpattau niyamaḥ kva cid eva yaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par

\chapter[{3.5 guṇasamuddeśaḥ}][{3.5 guṇasamuddeśaḥ}]{ 3.5 guṇasamuddeśaḥ}
	  
	

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	saṃsargi bhedakaṃ yad yat savyāpāraṃ pratīyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	guṇatvaṃ paratantratvāt tasya śāstra udāhṛtam 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.5.2 dravyasyāvyapadeśasya ya upādīyate guṇaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	bhedako vyapadeśāya tatprakarṣo+abhidhīyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.5.3 sarvasyaiva pradhānasya na vinā bhedahetunā 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	prakarṣo vidyate nāpi śabdasyopaiti vācyatām 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.5.4 vidyamānāḥ pradhāneṣu na sarve bhedahetavaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	viśeṣaśabdair ucyante vyāvṛttārthābhidhāyibhiḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.5.5 vastūpalakṣaṇe tatra viśeṣo vyāpṛto yadi 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	prakarṣo niyamābhāvāt syād avijñātahetukaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.5.6 sarvaṃ ca sarvato+avaśyaṃ niyamena prakṛṣyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	saṃsargiṇā nimittena nikṛṣṭenādhikena vā 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.5.7 nāpekṣate nimittaṃ ca prakarṣe vyāpṛtaṃ yadi 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	dravyasya syād upādānaṃ prakarṣaṃ praty anarthakam 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.5.8 savyāpāro guṇas tasmāt svaprakarṣanibandhanaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	dravyātmānaṃ bhinatty eva svaprakarṣaṃ niveśayan 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.5.9 arūpaṃ pararūpeṇa dravyam ākhyāyate yathā 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	aprakarṣaṃ prakarṣeṇa guṇasyāviśyate tathā 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	iti guṇasamuddeśaḥ
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par

\chapter[{3.6 diksamuddeśaḥ}][{3.6 diksamuddeśaḥ}]{ 3.6 diksamuddeśaḥ}

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.6.1 dik sādhanaṃ kriyā kāla iti vastvabhidhāyinaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	śaktirūpe padārthānām atyantam anavasthitāḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.6.2 vyatirekasya yo hetur avadhipratipādyayoḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	ṛjv ity evaṃ yato+anyena vinā buddhiḥ pravartate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.6.3 karmaṇo jātibhedānām abhivyaktir yadāśrayā 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	sā svair upādhibhir bhinnā śaktir dig iti kathyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.6.4 parāparatve mūrtīnāṃ deśabhedanibandhane 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	tata eva prakalpete kramarūpe tu kālataḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par

	3.6.5 ākāśasya pradeśena bhāgaiś cānyaiḥ pṛthak pṛthak

	\pend% ending standard par

	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par

	\pend% ending standard par

\chapter[{3.7 sādhanasamuddeśaḥ}][{3.7 sādhanasamuddeśaḥ}]{ 3.7 sādhanasamuddeśaḥ}

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.7.1 svāśraye samavetānāṃ tadvad evāśrayāntare 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	kriyāṇām abhiniṣpattau sāmarthyaṃ sādhanaṃ viduḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.7.2 śaktimā trāsam ūhasya viśvasyānekadharmaṇaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	sarvadā sarvathā bhāvāt kva cit kiṃ cid vivakṣyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.7.3 sādhanavyavahāraś ca buddhyavasthānibandhanaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	sann asan vārtharūpeṣu bhedo buddhyā prakalpyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.7.4 buddhyā samīhitaikatvān pañcālān kurubhir yadā 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	punar vibhajate vaktā tadāpāyaḥ pratīyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.7.5 śabdopahitarūpāṃś ca buddher viṣayatāṃ gatān 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	pratyakṣam iva kaṃsādīn sādhanatvena manyate

	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.7.6 buddhipravṛttirūpaṃ ca samāropyābhidhātṛbhiḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	artheṣu śaktibhedānāṃ kriyate parikalpanā 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.7.7 vyaktau padārthe śabdāder janyamānasya karmaṇaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	sādhanatvaṃ tathā siddhaṃ buddhirūpaprakalpitam

	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.7.8 svatantraparatantratve kramarūpaṃ ca darśitam

	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	nirīheṣv api bhāveṣu kalpanopanibandhanam

	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.7.9 śaktayaḥ śaktimantaś ca sarve saṃsargavādinām

	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	bhāvās teṣv asvaśabdeṣu sādhanatvaṃ nirūpyate

	niyatagrahaṇā loke śaktayas tās tathāśrayaiḥ

	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.7.17 pūrvasmin yā kriyā saiva parasmin sādhanaṃ matā

	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.7.18 niṣpattimātre kartṛtvaṃ sarvatraivāsti kārake

	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	vyāpārabhedāpekṣāyāṃ karaṇatvādisaṃbhavaḥ

	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.7.19 putrasya janmani yathā pitroḥ kartṛtvam ucyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	ayam asyām iyaṃ tv asmād iti bhedo vivakṣayā

	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.7.20 guṇakriyāṇāṃ kartāraḥ kartrā nyakkṛtaśaktayaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	nyaktāyām api saṃpūrṇaiḥ svair vyāpāraiḥ samanvitāḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.7.21 karaṇatvādibhir jñātāḥ kriyābhedānupātibhiḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	svātantryam uttaraṃ labdhvā pradhāne yānti kartṛtām 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.7.22 yathā rājñā niyukteṣu yoddhṛtvaṃ yoddhṛṣu sthitam 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	teṣu vṛttau tu labhate rājā jayaparājayau 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.7.23 tathā kartrā niyukteṣu sarveṣv ekārthakāriṣu 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	kartṛtvaṃ karaṇatvāder uttaraṃ na virudhyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.7.24 anāśrite tu vyāpāre nimittaṃ hetur iṣyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par

\chapter[{3.9: kālasamuddeśaḥ}][{3.9: kālasamuddeśaḥ}]{ 3.9: kālasamuddeśaḥ}

	3.9.1 vyāpāravyatirekeṇa kālam eke pracakṣate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	nityam ekaṃ vibhu dravyaṃ parimāṇaṃ kriyāvatām

\chapter[{3.10: puruṣasamuddeśa}][{3.10: puruṣasamuddeśa}]{ 3.10: puruṣasamuddeśa}

\chapter[{3.11: saṃkhyāsamuddeśa}][{3.11: saṃkhyāsamuddeśa}]{ 3.11: saṃkhyāsamuddeśa}

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.11.1 saṃkhyāvān sattvabhūto+arthaḥ sarva evābhidhīyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	bhedābhedavibhāgo hi loke saṃkhyānibandhanaḥ

	\pend% ending standard par

	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	bhedahetutvam āśritya saṃkhyeti vyapadiśyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.11.3 samavetā paricchedye kva cid anyatra sā sthitā 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	prakalpayati bhāvānāṃ saṃkhyā bhedaṃ tathātmanaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.11.4 paratve cāparatve ca bhede tulyā śrutir yathā 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	saṃkhyāśabdābhidheyatvaṃ bhedahetos tathā guṇe 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.11.5 asvatantre svatantratvaṃ paradharmo yathā guṇe 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par

	abhedye bhedyabhāvo+api dravyadharmas tathā guṇe

\chapter[{3.12: upagrahasamuddeśa}][{3.12: upagrahasamuddeśa}]{ 3.12: upagrahasamuddeśa}

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.12.1 ya ātmanepadād bhedaḥ kva cid arthasya gamyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	anyataś cāpi lādeśān manyante tam upagraham

	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.12.2 kva cit sādhanam evāsau kva cit tasya viśeṣaṇam 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	sādhanaṃ tatra karmādi vyaktavāco viśeṣaṇam

	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par

	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	lādeśaiḥ sa kriyābhedo vākyeṣv api niyamyate

	\pend% ending standard par

	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	plakṣaśabdasya sāṃnidhyān nyagrodhe plakṣatā yathā

	\pend% ending standard par

\chapter[{3.14: vṛttisamuddeśa}][{3.14: vṛttisamuddeśa}]{3.14: vṛttisamuddeśa}

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.1 kutsāpraśaṃsātiśayaiḥ samāptārthaṃ tu yujyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	padaṃ svārthādayaḥ sarve yasmāt kutsādihetavaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.2 devadattādikutsāyāṃ vartate kutsitaśrutiḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	kutsitasthā tu yā kutsā tadarthaḥ ko vidhīyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.3 prakṛṣṭa iti śuklādi- prakarṣasyābhidhāyakaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	prakṛṣṭasya prakarṣe tu tarabādir vidhīyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.4 kutsitatvena kutsyo vā na samyag vāpi kutsitaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	svaśabdābhihite kena viśiṣṭo+arthaḥ pratīyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.5 na ca sāṃpratikī kutsā bhedābhāvāt pratīyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	pūjyate kutsitatvena praśastatvena kutsyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.6 viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvaṃ padayor upajāyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	na prātipadikārthaś ca tatraiva vyatiricyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.7 viśeṣyaṃ syād anirjñātaṃ nirjñāto+artho viśeṣaṇam 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	parārthatvena śeṣatvaṃ sarveṣām upakāriṇām 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.8 vibhaktibhedo niyamād guṇaguṇyabhidhāyinoḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	sāmānādhikaraṇyasya prasiddhir dravyaśabdayoḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.9 dravye+anirjñātajātīye kṛṣṇaśabdaḥ prayujyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	anirjñātaguṇe caivaṃ tilaśabdaḥ pravartate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.10 sāmānyānām asaṃbandhāt tau viśeṣe vyavasthitau 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	rūpābhedād viśeṣaṃ tam abhivyaṅktuṃ na śaknutaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.11 tāv eva saṃnipatitau bhedena pratipādane 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par

	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	arthabhedo lubanteṣu naivaṃ kaś cana dṛśyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.599 yeṣūpameyavacanaḥ śabdo+anyo na prayujyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	upamānasya tatrānyaiḥ saṃkhyāyā bheda iṣyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.600 yathā guḍatilādīnāṃ prayogād ekasaṃkhyatā 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	pākāder aprayoge tu bhinnā saṃkhyābhidhīyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.601 yaḥ saṃbandhigato bhedaḥ sa prayoge pratīyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	saṃbandhinām ato bheda upameye na gamyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.602 tasmāt sāmānyaśabdatva-   prasaṅgavinivṛttaye 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	upameyagato bheda upamāneṣu dṛśyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.603 upamānaṃ samastānām abhinnam śrūyate kva cit 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	bhinnānām upameyanām ekaikam vopamīyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.604 yathā garuḍa ity etad vyūhāpekṣaṃ prayujyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	ekena yatra sādṛśyaṃ vainateyena hastinām 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.605 ekasyāpi pratīyeta bhinnā pratikṛtiḥ saha 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	kāśyapasyeti tenāyaṃ pratyekam avatiṣṭhate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.606 meghāḥ śaila ivety ukte samastānāṃ pratīyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	sādṛśyam giriṇaikena pratyekaṃ tena bhidyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.607 chāpekṣā tadviṣayatā vidheyatvān na gamyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	kākatālīyam ity atra prasiddham hy upalakṣaṇam 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.608 rājāśvādiś ca viṣayaḥ syād anyo vety aniścitam 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	tena cchasya vidhānāt prāg vyapadeśo na vidyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.609 dvayor ivārthayor atra nimittatvaṃ pratīyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	ekenāvayavo yuktaḥ pratyayo+anyena yujyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.610 caitrasya tatrāgamanaṃ kākasyāgamanaṃ yathā 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	dasyor abhinipātas tu tālasya patanaṃ yathā 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.611 saṃnipāte tayor yānyā kriyā tatropajāyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	vadhādir upameye+arthe tayā chavidhir iṣyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.612 kriyāyāṃ samavetāyāṃ dravyaśabdo +avatiṣṭhate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	pātāgamanayoḥ kāka- tālaśabdau tathā sthitau 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.613 yad anvākhyāyakaṃ vākyaṃ tad evaṃ parikalpyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	prayogavākvaṃ yal loke tad evaṃ na prayujyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.614 yayor atarkitā prāptir dṛśyate kākatālavat 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	tayoḥ samāsaprakṛter vṛttir abhyupagamyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.615 kākasya tālena yathā vadho yasya tu dasyunā 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	tatra citrīkṛte+anyasminn upameye cha iṣyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.616 cañcatprakāraś cañcatko bṛhatka iti cāpare 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	maṇimaḍḍūkakhadyotān sādṛśvena pracakṣate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.617 tatronmeṣanimeṣābhyāṃ khadyota upamīyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	śvāsaprabandhair maṇḍūkaḥ spandamānaprabho maṇiḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.618 pravikāsiprabho+alpo+api mahān ya upalabhyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	bṛhatka iti tatraiṣa maṇau śabdaḥ prayujyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.619 sādṛśyam eva sarvatra prakāraḥ kaiś cid iṣyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	bhede+api tu prakārākhyā kaiś cid abhyupagamyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.620 prakāravacanaḥ kaś cit prakāravati saṃsthitaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	prakāramātre vartitvā kaś cit tadvati vartate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.621 sādṛśyagrahaṇaṃ sūtre sadṛśasyopalakṣaṇam 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	tulyayor avyayībhāve sahaśabdo+abhidhāyakaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.622 vipsāsādṛśyayor vṛttir yā yathārthābhidhāyinaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	sa cāyam avyayībhāve bhedo bhedena darśitaḥ 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.623 sādṛśyaṃ yogyatā kaiś cid anāv abhyupagamyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	yat tu mūrtigataṃ sāmyaṃ tat sahenābhidhīyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.624 itthaṃbhāve+api sādṛśyaṃ   buddhyavasthānibandhanam 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	grahaṇe bhedamātrasya tatrānyaivābhidhīyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	3.14.625 gaur vāhīka iti dvitve sādṛśyaṃ pratyudāhṛtam 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      

	  
	  \pstart \leavevmode% starting standard par
	śuklādau sati niṣpanne vāhīko na dvir ucyate 
	{\color{gray}{\rmlatinfont\textsuperscript{§~\theparCount}}}
	\pend% ending standard par
      
		
		\pstart
		\begin{center}
	      iti bhartṛharikṛtaṃ vākyapadīyam samāptam
		\end{center}
		\pend

   <encodingDesc>
      <p>The electronic text below is in a lossless transliteration using the Latin alphabet.
                The transliteration scheme used is the IAST (<ref target="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Alphabet_of_Sanskrit_Transliteration">The International Alphabet of Sanskrit Transliteration</ref>). IAST differs in
                small ways from ISO 15919, but is preferred by most working Sanskrit scholars.
                Conversion of this file to ISO 15919 can be achieved by performing the following
                replacements throughout the file: <code> ṛ -&gt; r̥ and ṃ -&gt; ṁ </code>
            </p>
      <p>Text divison separates words with spaces ("ity evam" not "ityevam"), where sandhi
                permits.</p>
      <p>Avagraha is represented by +a. Thus "so 'pi" -&gt; "so+api".</p>
   </encodingDesc>
